## Specialization effectiveness

All entries are execution counts. Should add up to the total number of
Tier 1 instructions executed.

Basic

<td align="right">61.2%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">
Not specialized
<details>

</details>

<td align="right">3.6%</td>
</tr>

<td align="right">0.7%</td>
</tr>
